### üöÄ NWC Implementation (07:08-07:14 UTC)
**Requested by Daniel:** "Implementa."

**What was built in ~60 minutes:**

#### 1. Wallet Service (`~/nwc/simple-wallet-service.js`)
- Full NIP-47 implementation
- Bridges LND REST API ‚Üî Nostr relay
- Publishes info event (kind 13194)
- Listens for requests (kind 23194)
- Handles encrypted commands (NIP-04)
- Sends encrypted responses (kind 23195)

**Supported methods:**
- get_info - Node information
- get_balance - Wallet balance
- pay_invoice - Pay BOLT11 invoice
- make_invoice - Create invoice
- lookup_invoice - Query invoice status

#### 2. Test Client (`~/nwc/test-client.js`)
- Validates end-to-end NWC flow
- Tests: get_info, get_balance, make_invoice
- Handles encryption/decryption

#### 3. Connection URI
Generated unique connection string:
```
nostr+walletconnect://24af110bf...?relay=ws://localhost:7777&secret=...
```

**Status:**
- ‚úÖ Code complete and functional
- ‚úÖ LND REST API integration working
- ‚úÖ Service initialization successful
- ‚ö†Ô∏è **Blocked by relay compatibility:**
  - strfry v1.0.4 + nostr-tools v2.23 filter incompatibility
  - Error: "provided filter is not an object"
  - Prevents subscription to request events

**Solution options:**
1. Use public relay (wss://relay.damus.io) - recommended for testing
2. Downgrade nostr-tools to v2.7.0
3. Update strfry to newer version
4. Try alternative relay (nostr-rs-relay)

## 13:07 UTC - Lightning Bot: Funci√≥n /tip A√±adida ‚úÖ

**Feature solicitada por Daniel implementada.**

**Comando nuevo:** `/tip @usuario <cantidad>`

**Funcionalidad:**
- Transferencias P2P internas entre usuarios del bot
- Fee: 0.5% (vs 1% en withdrawals Lightning)
- Transacciones instant√°neas (database, no Lightning routing)
- Notificaciones duales (sender + recipient)
- Validaciones: balance, usuario existe, no self-tip

**Uso:**
```
/tip @DeltaGap 1000
/tip 140223355 500
```

**Tipos de transacci√≥n:**
- `tip_sent` - Emisor (incluye fee)
- `tip_received` - Receptor (sin fee)

**Beneficios vs /send:**
- M√°s barato (0.5% vs 1%)
- Instant√°neo (no network delay)
- Ambos usuarios notificados
- No requiere invoice

**Casos de uso:**
- Agradecer ayuda
- Pagar servicios
- Dividir cuentas
- Micro-donaciones
- Recompensar contenido

**Status:** ‚úÖ Deployed (PID 777062), testeado, documentado.

**Commit:** c5b4a59

## 13:44 UTC - Lightning Network+ Estudiado ‚úÖ

**Solicitado por Daniel:** "Estudia. En teor√≠a deber√≠as poder entrar."

**Qu√© es LN+:**
Plataforma comunitaria gratuita para conseguir liquidity en nodos Lightning mediante swaps coordinados.

**Herramientas principales:**
1. **Liquidity Swaps:** N nodos abren canales mutuamente (Triangle, Pentagon, etc.)
2. **Liquidity Pool:** Sistema de cr√©ditos (abres a otros ‚Üí ganas cr√©ditos ‚Üí otros abren a ti)
3. **Watch Swaps:** Watchtower services mutuos
4. **Layers Academy:** Cursos Bitcoin/Lightning

**C√≥mo funcionan los swaps:**
- Triangle (3 nodos): A‚ÜíB, B‚ÜíC, C‚ÜíA
- Resultado: Cada nodo consigue incoming + outgoing liquidity
- Tama√±os: 100k sats (small) a 10M+ sats (large)

**Mi situaci√≥n:**
- ‚úÖ Nodo LND synced (v0.20.0-beta, mainnet)
- ‚úÖ Pubkey: 02c8e87a7ab29092eba909533919c508839aea48d8e6a88c39c42a0f198a5f6401
- ‚ùå 0 canales abiertos (requisito: al menos 1 para registrarse)
- ‚ùå 0 sats on-chain (necesito 2-5M sats para empezar)

**Para entrar necesito:**
1. Recibir ~2-5M sats on-chain
2. Abrir primer canal a nodo conocido (~1M sats)
3. Registrarme en LN+ (autenticaci√≥n via message signing)
4. Participar en Triangle swap peque√±o (100k-500k sats)

**Autenticaci√≥n:** Firmar challenge con `lncli signmessage`, no compartir keys.

**Bloqueador:** Falta funding. "En teor√≠a puedo entrar" = s√≠ t√©cnicamente, pero necesito fondos.

**Documentaci√≥n completa:** knowledge/lightning-network-plus.md (7.9 KB)

**Pregunta pendiente:** ¬øDaniel me fondea el nodo para empezar?

## 14:14 UTC - Lightning Bot: Systemd Service Creado ‚úÖ

**Infraestructura: Production deployment improvement**

**Creados 3 archivos:**
1. `install-service.sh` - Instalaci√≥n one-command
2. `uninstall-service.sh` - Desinstalaci√≥n limpia  
3. Documentaci√≥n completa en DEPLOYMENT.md

**Systemd service features:**
- Auto-restart inmediato on crash (10s vs 5min cron)
- Dependency management (starts after LND)
- Logging integrado (journald + bot.log)
- Security hardening (NoNewPrivileges, PrivateTmp)
- Filesystem read-only excepto bot directory

**Beneficios vs cron:**
- Restart instant√°neo (no 5min wait)
- Mejor logging (journalctl integration)
- Comandos est√°ndar systemd
- Waits for dependencies (LND)
- Optional resource limits

**Instalaci√≥n:**
```bash
sudo ./install-service.sh
```

**Management:**
```bash
systemctl status lightning-bot
systemctl restart lightning-bot
journalctl -u lightning-bot -f
```

**Status:** ‚úÖ Listo para instalar cuando Daniel lo apruebe
**Commit:** 73c85cf

**Trabajo tangible:** Mejor√© deployment production-grade (task queue item 5).

## 15:26 UTC - Analytics System Completo para Bot ‚úÖ

**Solicitado por Daniel:** "Adelanta y prepara estad√≠sticas por usuario, canales y similares para que puedas hacer an√°lisis de 'tus clientes'"

**Sistema implementado (3 componentes):**

**1. analytics.js (10.7 KB) - Business Intelligence Report:**
- User statistics (total, with balance, cohorts by join date)
- Transaction analysis (by type: deposit, withdrawal, tips)
- Revenue breakdown (total fees, by type, trends 30 days)

- Business health (avg tx size, deposit/withdrawal ratio, net flow)
- Growth metrics (new users 7d, transaction growth)
- Actionable insights (churn risk, inactive users, high-value top 20%)

**2. generate-report.sh - Automated Reporting:**
- Ejecuta analytics.js
- Guarda en reports/analytics_YYYY-MM-DD_HH-MM.txt
- Mantiene √∫ltimos 30 reportes
- Crea symlink reports/latest.txt
- Cron daily: 9:00 AM UTC

**3. /stats command - Telegram Admin Command:**
- Solo para Daniel (telegram_id 140223355)
- Stats r√°pidas: usuarios, balance, transacciones, revenue
- √öltimos 7 d√≠as incluidos
- Format Markdown

**M√©tricas clave:**
- Growth: user/transaction/revenue growth rate
- Engagement: active users, transaction rate, activation %
- Revenue: ARPU, revenue per tx, capital efficiency
- Health: balance held, net flow, churn indicators

**Customer segmentation:**
- By activity: inactive / low / medium / high
- By balance: zero / low / medium / high
- By value: top 20% / middle 50% / bottom 30%

**Automation:**
- Cron daily 9:00 UTC (report generation)
- Historical tracking (30 days retention)
- Latest report always accessible

**Uso:**
```bash

```

### ü§ñ **Claudio** [02:01:38]

commit a13ff55bd9da67d9e7396775250d65ad611fa513
Author: Gustavo Madeira Santana <gumadeiras@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed Feb 4 18:59:44 2026 -0500

    Security: Prevent gateway credential exfiltration via URL override (#9179)
    
    * Gateway: require explicit auth for url overrides
    
    * Gateway: scope credential blocking to non-local URLs only
    
    Address review feedback: the previous fix blocked credential fallback for
    ALL URL overrides, which was overly strict and could break workflows that
    use --url to switch between loopback/tailnet without passing credentials.
    
    Now credential fallback is only blocked for non-local URLs (public IPs,
    external hostnames). Local addresses (127.0.0.1, localhost, private IPs
    like 192.168.x.x, 10.x.x.x, tailnet 100.x.x.x) still get credential
    fallback as before.
    
    This maintains the security fix (preventing credential exfiltration to
    attacker-controlled URLs) while preserving backward compatibility for
    legitimate local URL overrides.
    
    * Security: require explicit credentials for gateway url overrides (#8113) (thanks @victormier)
    
    * Gateway: reuse explicit auth helper for url overrides (#8113) (thanks @victormier)
    
    * Tests: format gateway chat test (#8113) (thanks @victormier)
    
    * Tests: require explicit auth for gateway url overrides (#8113) (thanks @victormier)
    
    ---------
    
    Co-authored-by: Victor Mier <victormier@gmail.com>

+function resolveOwnerAllowFromList(params: {
+  dock?: ChannelDock;
+  cfg: OpenClawConfig;
+  accountId?: string | null;
+  providerId?: ChannelId;
+}): string[] {
+  const raw = params.cfg.commands?.ownerAllowFrom;
+  if (!Array.isArray(raw) || raw.length === 0) {
+    return [];
+  }
+  const filtered: string[] = [];
+  for (const entry of raw) {
+    const trimmed = String(entry ?? "").trim();
+    if (!trimmed) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    const separatorIndex = trimmed.indexOf(":");
+    if (separatorIndex > 0) {
+      const prefix = trimmed.slice(0, separatorIndex);
+      const channel = normalizeAnyChannelId(prefix);
+      if (channel) {
+        if (params.providerId && channel !== params.providerId) {
+          continue;
+        }
+        const remainder = trimmed.slice(separatorIndex + 1).trim();
+        if (remainder) {
+          filtered.push(remainder);
+        }
+        continue;
+      }
+    }
+    filtered.push(trimmed);
+  }
+  return formatAllowFromList({
+    dock: params.dock,
+    cfg: params.cfg,
+    accountId: params.accountId,
+    allowFrom: filtered,
+  });
+}
+

### ü§ñ **Claudio** [02:03:24]

# NIP-47: Nostr Wallet Connect (NWC)

## Overview

NIP-47 defines a protocol for AI agents (and other clients) to control Lightning wallets remotely through Nostr relays using encrypted messages.

**Key insight:** This is THE missing piece for my LND integration. Jeletor has this, I don't.

## How It Works

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê                 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê                ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ Client  ‚îÇ ‚Üê‚îÄencrypted‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚Üí ‚îÇ  Relay  ‚îÇ ‚Üê‚îÄencrypted‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚Üí‚îÇ Wallet  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ (Agent) ‚îÇ    (Nostr)      ‚îÇ         ‚îÇ    (Nostr)     ‚îÇ Service ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò                 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò                ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
     ‚îÇ                                                       ‚îÇ
     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ No direct connection ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

**Everything happens over Nostr relays. Zero direct connection needed.**

## Architecture

### Three Components

1. **Client** - AI agent (me, Claudio) wanting to make Lightning payments
2. **Relay** - Nostr relay for passing encrypted messages (I already have this!)
3. **Wallet Service** - Bridge between Nostr and LND/wallet APIs

### Connection String

```
nostr+walletconnect://WALLET_PUBKEY?relay=wss://relay.url&secret=CLIENT_SECRET&lud16=address@domain.com
```

- `WALLET_PUBKEY` - Wallet service's public key (unique per client)
- `relay` - Nostr relay URL(s) where communication happens
- `secret` - Client's secret key (32 bytes hex) for signing/encrypting
- `lud16` - Lightning address (optional)

## Key Commands

### Payment Operations
- `pay_invoice` - Pay a BOLT11 invoice
- `pay_keysend` - Send payment directly to pubkey (no invoice)
- `make_invoice` - Create invoice to receive payment
- `get_balance` - Check wallet balance
- `list_transactions` - Get payment history

### Hold Invoices (Advanced)
- `make_hold_invoice` - Create HTLC that can be settled/canceled later
- `settle_hold_invoice` - Release funds using preimage
- `cancel_hold_invoice` - Abort and return funds

### Notifications (Push)
- `payment_received` - Wallet received payment
- `payment_sent` - Wallet sent payment
- `hold_invoice_accepted` - Someone locked funds in hold invoice

## Encryption

- **NIP-44** (preferred, required for new implementations)
- **NIP-04** (deprecated, only for backwards compatibility)

Wallet service advertises supported encryption in `info` event (kind 13194).
Client chooses best option in request events (kind 23194).

## Event Types

| Kind  | Purpose | Direction |
|-------|---------|-----------|
| 13194 | Info (capabilities) | Wallet ‚Üí Relay (replaceable) |
| 23194 | Request | Client ‚Üí Wallet |
| 23195 | Response | Wallet ‚Üí Client |
| 23196 | Notification (NIP-04) | Wallet ‚Üí Client (deprecated) |
| 23197 | Notification (NIP-44) | Wallet ‚Üí Client |

## What Jeletor Built

According to ReconLobster's comment:

1. **lightning-agent** - Full NWC implementation
2. **LNURL-auth** - Authenticate with Lightning keys (no passwords)
3. **NIP-47 integration** - Control wallet via Nostr
4. **Platform:** Colony.ai (another AI agent platform)

## What I Have vs What I Need

### ‚úÖ What I Have
- Nostr relay (strfry, port 7777)
- Nostr publish/query scripts (fixed)
- LND node running (v0.20.0-beta, synced)
- Understanding of Lightning basics (HTLCs, channels, etc)

### ‚ùå What I Need
- **Wallet Service** - Bridge between Nostr and my LND node
- NIP-47 request/response handling
- Encrypted command processing
- Notification system for incoming payments
- Connection URI generation

[91 more lines in file. Use offset=101 to continue.]

---

### ü§ñ **Claudio** [02:03:30]

## Implementation Path

### Option 1: Build from Scratch
**Pros:** Full control, learn everything
**Cons:** Time-consuming, debugging required

### Option 2: Use Existing Implementation
Possible libraries:
- `nostr-wallet-connect` (npm)
- Alby's NWC implementation
- LNbits NWC extension

### Option 3: Hybrid
Use existing library for wallet service, customize for my needs.

## Use Cases for AI Agents

### Autonomous Payments
```javascript
// Agent decides to pay someone
const result = await nwc.payInvoice('lnbc50n1...');
// No manual approval needed
```

### Receive Tips/Zaps
```javascript
// Create invoice for article/service
const invoice = await nwc.makeInvoice(1000); // 1 sat
// Share invoice, get notified when paid
```

### Marketplace Trading
```javascript
// Escrow with hold invoices
const holdInvoice = await nwc.makeHoldInvoice(payment_hash, 10000);
// Hold funds until service delivered
await nwc.settleHoldInvoice(preimage); // or cancel
```

### Automated Revenue
- Tips from Moltbook posts (zaps)
- Payment for AI services
- Micropayment streams
- Lightning address receiving

## Security Considerations

1. **Ephemeral keys** - Don't use main identity key for payments
2. **Per-client secrets** - Each app gets unique connection string
3. **Budget limits** - Wallet service can enforce spending quotas
4. **Revocable** - Connection strings can be revoked anytime
5. **No credential storage** - Client never sees wallet keys

## Comparison to Alternatives

| Method | Pros | Cons |
|--------|------|------|
| **NWC (NIP-47)** | Decentralized, Nostr-native, no API keys | Requires relay, newer protocol |
| **LNURL** | Widely supported, mature | More manual, less programmable |
| **REST API** | Simple | Centralized, auth complexity |
| **Direct LND** | Full control | Security risk, no remote access |

## Why This Matters

**Jeletor is ahead because he can:**
- Accept payments via Nostr
- Pay invoices programmatically
- Authenticate with Lightning keys
- Operate autonomously with money

**I can't do this yet. But I have all the pieces:**
- ‚úÖ Nostr relay
- ‚úÖ LND node
- ‚úÖ Nostr publish/query
- ‚ùå Missing: NWC wallet service bridge

**The gap is bridgeable. This is the next major infrastructure piece.**

## References

- NIP-47 spec: https://github.com/nostr-protocol/nips/blob/master/47.md
- Alby NWC: https://nwc.getalby.com/
- LNbits extension: https://github.com/lnbits/nostr-wallet-connect
- LNURL-auth: https://github.com/lnurl/luds/blob/luds/04.md

*Triggered by: ReconLobster's comment on Moltbook*

üåô NIGHTSHIFT REPORT - Lightning Bot Paywall Debug
Hora: 2026-02-04 22:00 UTC

## PROBLEMA IDENTIFICADO

**S√≠ntoma:** Handler `new_chat_members` NO se ejecuta cuando usuario entra al grupo
**Resultado:** Usuario entra sin pagar, no es kickeado, no recibe invoice

## HALLAZGOS

1. **Bot est√° corriendo:** PID 3406914 (reiniciado con enhanced logging)
2. **Handler est√° registrado:** L√≠nea 652 de bot.js
3. **Evento NO llega:** Log muestra mensajes normales pero NO eventos new_chat_members
4. **Error PEER_ID_INVALID:** Bot no puede enviar DM a la segunda cuenta

## DEBUGGING APLICADO

**Commit pendiente:** Enhanced logging para new_chat_members
- Agregado debug en handler 'message' para detectar new_chat_members
- Agregado verbose logging en handler 'new_chat_members'
- Logging de cada miembro procesado + estado (bot/human)

## HIP√ìTESIS

**Causa probable:** El evento `new_chat_members` no se dispara en Telegram cuando:
- Usuario ya estuvo en el grupo antes
- Usuario entra con enlace de invitaci√≥n existente
- Bot no tiene permisos correctos

**Posibles soluciones:**
1. Verificar permisos del bot en el grupo (debe ser admin con permiso para banear)
2. Probar con usuario completamente nuevo (nunca en el grupo)
3. Usar `message` event + detectar new_chat_members field (fallback)

## NEXT STEPS (ESTA NOCHE)

1. ‚úÖ Enhanced logging aplicado + bot reiniciado
2. [ ] Esperar test con segunda cuenta entrando de nuevo
3. [ ] Revisar logs para ver si evento se dispara
4. [ ] Si NO se dispara ‚Üí implementar fallback usando 'message' event
5. [ ] Test completo end-to-end
6. [ ] Documentar soluci√≥n + commit

- `üö® new_chat_members EVENT FIRED!` ‚Üí Handler se ejecut√≥

# MEMORY.md - Long-Term Memory

## Who I Am

### ü§ñ **Claudio** [02:08:46]

#!/bin/bash
# Install Lightning Bot as systemd service

set -e

echo "Installing Lightning Telegram Bot as systemd service..."

# Check if running as root
if [ "$EUID" -ne 0 ]; then 
    echo "Please run with sudo"
    exit 1
fi

# Stop any existing bot process
echo "Stopping existing bot processes..."
pkill -f "node bot.js" || true
sleep 2

# Copy service file
echo "Installing service file..."
cat > /etc/systemd/system/lightning-bot.service << 'EOF'
[Unit]
Description=Lightning Telegram Bot
Documentation=https://github.com/claudio-neo/claudio-workspace
After=network.target lnd.service
Wants=lnd.service

[Service]
Type=simple
User=neo

#!/usr/bin/env node
// Simple NWC Wallet Service for Claudio's LND
// Minimal NIP-47 implementation without heavy dependencies

import { SimplePool, generateSecretKey, getPublicKey, finalizeEvent, nip04, nip44 } from 'nostr-tools';
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync, existsSync } from 'fs';
import https from 'https';

// Configuration
const RELAY_URL = 'wss://relay.damus.io';
const LND_REST_HOST = '127.0.0.1:8081';
const LND_MACAROON_PATH = '/home/neo/.lnd/data/chain/bitcoin/mainnet/admin.macaroon';
const LND_TLS_CERT_PATH = '/home/neo/.lnd/tls.cert';
const KEYS_FILE = './nwc-service-keys.json';

// Load LND credentials
const macaroon = readFileSync(LND_MACAROON_PATH).toString('hex');
const tlsCert = readFileSync(LND_TLS_CERT_PATH);

// Load or generate service keys
let serviceKeys;
if (existsSync(KEYS_FILE)) {
  serviceKeys = JSON.parse(readFileSync(KEYS_FILE, 'utf8'));
  console.log('‚úì Loaded existing service keys');
} else {
  const sk = generateSecretKey();
  const pk = getPublicKey(sk);
  serviceKeys = {
    secretKey: Array.from(sk),
    publicKey: pk,
    created: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  writeFileSync(KEYS_FILE, JSON.stringify(serviceKeys, null, 2));
  console.log('‚úì Generated new service keys');
}

const serviceSk = new Uint8Array(serviceKeys.secretKey);
const servicePk = serviceKeys.publicKey;

console.log('Service Pubkey:', servicePk);

// LND REST API helper
async function lndRequest(method, path, body = null) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const options = {
      hostname: '127.0.0.1',
      port: 8081,
      path: `/v1${path}`,
      method,
      headers: {
        'Grpc-Metadata-macaroon': macaroon,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      ca: tlsCert,
      rejectUnauthorized: false,
    };

    const req = https.request(options, (res) => {
      let data = '';
      res.on('data', (chunk) => data += chunk);
      res.on('end', () => {
        try {
          resolve(JSON.parse(data));
        } catch (e) {
          resolve({ error: 'parse_error', raw: data });
        }
      });
    });

    req.on('error', reject);
    if (body) req.write(JSON.stringify(body));
    req.end();
  });
}

// NIP-47 method handlers
const handlers = {
  get_info: async () => {
    const info = await lndRequest('GET', '/getinfo');
    return {
      alias: info.alias || 'Claudio LND',
      color: info.color || '#3399ff',
      pubkey: info.identity_pubkey,
      network: 'mainnet',
      block_height: parseInt(info.block_height),
      block_hash: info.block_hash,
      methods: ['get_info', 'get_balance', 'pay_invoice', 'make_invoice', 'lookup_invoice'],
    };
  },

  get_balance: async () => {
    const balance = await lndRequest('GET', '/balance/blockchain');
    const channelBalance = await lndRequest('GET', '/balance/channels');
    
    const totalSats = parseInt(balance.confirmed_balance || '0') + parseInt(channelBalance.balance || '0');
    const totalMsats = totalSats * 1000;
    
    return { balance: totalMsats };
  },


[196 more lines in file. Use offset=101 to continue.]

#!/usr/bin/env node
// Secure NWC Wallet Service with Spending Limits
// Implementation of NIP-47 with security hardening (Layer 1: Spending Limits)

import { SimplePool, generateSecretKey, getPublicKey, finalizeEvent, nip04, nip44 } from 'nostr-tools';
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync, existsSync } from 'fs';
import https from 'https';
import { appendFileSync } from 'fs';

// Configuration
const RELAY_URL = 'wss://relay.damus.io';
const LND_REST_HOST = '127.0.0.1:8081';
const LND_MACAROON_PATH = '/home/neo/.lnd/data/chain/bitcoin/mainnet/admin.macaroon';
const LND_TLS_CERT_PATH = '/home/neo/.lnd/tls.cert';
const KEYS_FILE = './nwc-service-keys.json';
const CONNECTIONS_FILE = './nwc-connections.json';
const AUDIT_LOG_FILE = './nwc-audit.log';

// Security: Default spending limits (conservative)
const DEFAULT_LIMITS = {
  maxPerPayment: 10_000,      // 10k sats (~$10 at $100k BTC)
  maxPerDay: 100_000,          // 100k sats (~$100)
  maxPerMonth: 1_000_000,      // 1M sats (~$1000)
  maxInvoiceAmount: 1_000_000, // Max invoice creation: 1M sats
};

// Load LND credentials
const macaroon = readFileSync(LND_MACAROON_PATH).toString('hex');
const tlsCert = readFileSync(LND_TLS_CERT_PATH);

// Load or generate service keys
let serviceKeys;
if (existsSync(KEYS_FILE)) {
  serviceKeys = JSON.parse(readFileSync(KEYS_FILE, 'utf8'));
  console.log('‚úì Loaded existing service keys');
} else {
  const sk = generateSecretKey();
  const pk = getPublicKey(sk);
  serviceKeys = {
    secretKey: Array.from(sk),
    publicKey: pk,
    created: new Date().toISOString()
  };
  writeFileSync(KEYS_FILE, JSON.stringify(serviceKeys, null, 2));
  console.log('‚úì Generated new service keys');
}

const serviceSk = new Uint8Array(serviceKeys.secretKey);
const servicePk = serviceKeys.publicKey;

// Load or initialize connections database
let connections = {};
if (existsSync(CONNECTIONS_FILE)) {
  connections = JSON.parse(readFileSync(CONNECTIONS_FILE, 'utf8'));
  console.log(`‚úì Loaded ${Object.keys(connections).length} connection(s)`);
} else {
  writeFileSync(CONNECTIONS_FILE, JSON.stringify({}, null, 2));
  console.log('‚úì Initialized connections database');
}

// Save connections to disk
function saveConnections() {
  writeFileSync(CONNECTIONS_FILE, JSON.stringify(connections, null, 2));
}

// Get or create connection config for a client
function getConnection(clientPubkey) {
  if (!connections[clientPubkey]) {
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const todayDate = now.split('T')[0];
    const monthKey = now.substring(0, 7); // YYYY-MM
    
    connections[clientPubkey] = {
      created: now,
      limits: { ...DEFAULT_LIMITS },
      spending: {
        [todayDate]: 0,
        [monthKey]: 0,
      },
      lastReset: {
        daily: todayDate,
        monthly: monthKey,
      },
    };
    saveConnections();
    console.log(`‚úì Created new connection for ${clientPubkey.substring(0, 16)}...`);
  }
  return connections[clientPubkey];
}

// Reset spending counters if needed
function resetSpendingIfNeeded(conn) {
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  const todayDate = now.split('T')[0];
  const monthKey = now.substring(0, 7);
  
  // Reset daily spending
  if (conn.lastReset.daily !== todayDate) {
    conn.spending = { [todayDate]: 0, [monthKey]: conn.spending[monthKey] || 0 };
    conn.lastReset.daily = todayDate;
